Modern Last Chance Trial Winning Decklists
==========================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on December 8, 2018 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_adamstyborski.jpg)
By Adam Styborski




 Stybs has played Magic the world over, writing and drafting as part of the event coverage team and slinging Commander everywhere his decks will fit. 






Among *Magic* players, Modern carries the reputation of being "anything goes" where popular decks live alongside the creative creations that become the next best deck. At Portland, there were 47 different players who claimed victory in a Last Chance Trial.


While below is a sample of the unique decklists that earned two byes, it's worth noting several are specifically popular across the Trial winners: Bant Spirits, Hardened Scales Affinity, Infect, Jeskai Control, Hollow One, Krark-Clan Ironworks, Dredge and Izzet Phoenix all of them had multiple winners.







#### Cameron Herzog's Izzet Phoenix


##### 






![Download Arena Decklist](https://web.archive.org/web/20211024134741im_/https://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download_arena.png)
![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
